The lobby is also very grand. As soon as I entered the door, a beautiful lady helped me push my luggage to the front desk and the elevator. She responded to every request: I asked if the air conditioner could be adjusted to a higher temperature. It couldn't be adjusted at first, but it was adjusted soon. The problem-solving ability was too strong. The slippers in the room also looked very advanced, different from ordinary disposable slippers. On the same day, several service staff also sent a plate of fruit with a smile. When I came back from climbing the mountain the next day, I found that the fruit was filled and I was given a pair of insoles. The sewer for taking a shower was blocked that day. After the response, the staff immediately smiled and checked it. The breakfast was also very rich, but I ate less, which was a bit regrettable! Overall, it is the best hotel I have stayed in! It is just too far from Mount Tai and the high-speed rail station.

name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Superior Room (2 beds)
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Family
info:1 Review
rating:5
posted:Posted April 6, 2024
msg:It was a very good experience. We came here in a hurry and decided to go on a spontaneous trip. It was not until the night before Qingming Festival that we decided to drive to Mount Tai for three days during the Qingming Festival. Although we didn't book a place closer to the Taishan Scenic Area, the unexpected encounter with Baosheng Daogu Hotel made this self-driving tour more comfortable. First of all, the hotel environment is very good, parking is also very convenient, and the distance from the scenic area is not far or near, so the trip is very smooth. We checked in on the first day of our self-driving trip and booked a two-night package (be sure to book a room on the west side in advance so that you can directly see the Jade Emperor Peak of Taishan). We also gave away tickets for the Fengshan Ceremony, which we arranged to watch that night. It was very good. The next morning, we drove to Tianwai Village to take the scenic area bus to Zhongtianmen and then climb up the mountain (a less strenuous way to climb with children). One thing to mention here is that the municipal government parking lot is free for tourists to park, which is very heartwarming. Although climbing the mountain is very tiring, returning to the hotel, the comfortable environment, the warm smiles of the staff and the attentive service will instantly sweep away the fatigue. By the way, the hotel buffet breakfast also has local specialty breakfast millet soup, which also saves the time to go to the old street to drink millet soup, and other content is also very rich. In short, this impromptu journey is an unforgettable experience. I also look forward to coming back next time to make up for the regret of not climbing the mountain to watch the sunrise.

msg:A very satisfying stay!!

Facilities: A new hotel, which has just opened for half a year and is gradually getting better. The lobby display and room layout are pretty good. I wonâ€™t say much about the similarities. The pillows are very comfortable. My family of three should all use the latex one, and they all said they slept well. The bathroom is particularly considerate and has a disposable bathtub bag (I just happened to bring this one myself this time), so I finally donâ€™t have to wash the bathtub to give the baby a bath, which is great!

Service: Also very good! 1. The package I booked is equipped with a king-size bed room. I originally called to inquire about how to pay if I want to upgrade the room type. The front desk MM (sorry for forgetting to ask her name, it was the sister who was on duty at the switchboard around 8 o'clock in the morning on 0225) was very enthusiastic. Not only did she write down my needs, but she also called me back several times, and finally applied for a free upgrade to a parent-child room for me! 2. We had a buffet dinner at the hotel. A staff member came to give gifts to the children. Because it was a small dinosaur toy, my daughter didn't like it and politely refused it. She was not unhappy. But the staff member went out of his way to find a shiny toy bracelet for my daughter, which made her very happy! 3. I called the customer service at about 9:30 pm to ask for a few bottles of mineral water. The response speed was super fast!

Location: It is very convenient to drive by yourself. It takes about ten minutes to get there on a straight road down the highway. We just passed by for one night and didn't go anywhere else. I roughly looked at the map and found that it was relatively close to Fantawild. My teammates said that it was six or seven kilometers to Mount Tai, which should be okay. When we walked, we saw that there was a Wuyue Commercial not far away.

Catering: The buffet dinner was actually quite good. Of course, it was not top-notch, but the richness and freshness of the dishes were OK. The grilled skewers and small seafood in sauce tasted very good. Each table was equipped with a pot. It was very warm to simmer some meat and fresh vegetables on this day. In comparison, the breakfast seemed to be more average, just average.

In general, as a place to rest for one night on the way back, I was very satisfied with this stay, and it received high praise from my teammates and kids!!
